| Goal | Tool |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes CRD Validation to OpenAPI Schema Publishing Chain

## Your Task

Trace how a CustomResourceDefinition's validation schema is converted to an OpenAPI schema in kubernetes/kubernetes. Find Go source files implementing: the CRD validation spec, the structural schema extraction, the OpenAPI v3 schema conversion, and the API server spec endpoint publication.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

### 3. OpenAPI Schema Conversion

- **`pkg/controller/openapi/v2/conversion.go`** — `ToStructuralOpenAPIV2()`: strips v2-incompatible constructs (allOf, oneOf, nullable)
- **`pkg/controller/openapi/builder/merge.go`** — `MergeSpecs()` / `MergeSpecsV3()`: merge per-CRD specs with static built-in API specs

CRD Validation Spec Definition\\n\\nThe CRD validation schema is defined in the API types:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/types.go` \u2014 internal `CustomResourceValidation` type with `OpenAPIV3Schema *JSONSchemaProps`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1/types.go` \u2014 v1 `CustomResourceValidation` type\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/v1beta1/types.go` \u2014 v1beta1 equivalent\\n\\nValidation of these schemas is done in:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/validation/validation.go` \u2014 validates CRD spec, requires structural schemas in v1\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/validation/cel_validation.go` \u2014 CEL rule validation within schemas\\n\\n## 2. Structural Schema Extraction\\n\\nThe structural schema package converts the JSONSchemaProps to an internal Structural representation:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/structural.go` \u2014 defines the `Structural` type\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/convert.go` \u2014 implements `NewStructural()` which converts `apiextensions.JSONSchemaProps` to `*Structural`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/validation.go` \u2014 implements `ValidateStructural()` which validates the structural schema\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/unfold.go` \u2014 implements `Unfold()` which expands ValueValidation (anyOf/allOf)\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/complete.go` \u2014 schema completion logic\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/skeleton.go` \u2014 structural skeleton construction\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/visitor.go` \u2014 visitor pattern for traversing structural schemas\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/kubeopenapi.go` \u2014 implements `ToKubeOpenAPI()` which converts a `Structural` back to a go-openapi `spec.Schema`\\n\\n## 3. OpenAPI V3 and V2 Schema Conversion\\n\\nThe conversion from Structural schema to OpenAPI spec is done in the builder:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapi/builder/builder.go` \u2014 contains `generateBuilder()`, `BuildOpenAPIV2()`, and `BuildOpenAPIV3()`. The `generateBuilder` function calls `apiextensionshelpers.GetSchemaForVersion()` to get the CRD schema, converts it to internal form, calls `NewStructural()`, then `Unfold()`, and optionally strips value validations. `BuildOpenAPIV2` and `BuildOpenAPIV3` then produce OpenAPI specs from the restful routes and schema.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapi/v2/conversion.go` \u2014 implements `ToStructuralOpenAPIV2()` which strips OpenAPI v2-incompatible fields (allOf, oneOf, anyOf, not, nullable, etc.) from the structural schema before calling `ToKubeOpenAPI()`.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapi/builder/merge.go` \u2014 implements `MergeSpecs()` (v2) and `MergeSpecsV3()` (v3) for merging per-version CRD specs together and with the static spec.\\n\\n## 4. API Server Spec Endpoint Publication\\n\\nThe controllers watch CRD changes and publish the OpenAPI specs:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapi/controller.go` \u2014 `Controller` (v2): watches CRD informer, calls `BuildOpenAPIV2` per version, merges specs, and calls `openAPIService.UpdateSpecLazy(cache)` to publish to the `/openapi/v2` endpoint\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapi/metrics.go` \u2014 metrics for OpenAPI v2 regeneration\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapiv3/controller.go` \u2014 `Controller` (v3): watches CRD informer, calls `BuildOpenAPIV3` per version, merges specs per GroupVersion, and calls `openAPIV3Service.UpdateGroupVersion(path, mergedSpec)` to publish to the `/openapi/v3` endpoint\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapiv3/metrics.go` \u2014 metrics for OpenAPI v3 regeneration\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapiv3/util.go` \u2014 utility for converting GroupVersion to OpenAPI v3 path (`apis/<group>/<version>`)\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/nonstructuralschema/nonstructuralschema_controller.go` \u2014 watches CRDs and sets the `NonStructuralSchema` condition, which gates OpenAPI publishing\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/apiserver.go` \u2014 wires everything together in the `start-apiextensions-controllers` post-start hook, launching both the v2 and v3 OpenAPI controllers using `GenericAPIServer.OpenAPIVersionedService` and `GenericAPIServer.OpenAPIV3VersionedService`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go` \u2014 uses structural schema for validation and schema-aware serving of custom resources\\n\\n## Complete Chain Summary\\n\\n1. `CustomResourceValidation.OpenAPIV3Schema` (in CRD spec, `v1/types.go`) is the input\\n2. `validation.go:ValidateCRDSpec()` validates the CRD including schema constraints (structural, types, CEL rules)\\n3. `convert.go:NewStructural()` converts `JSONSchemaProps` to `*Structural` (the internal structural representation)\\n4. `validation.go:ValidateStructural()` confirms it is a valid structural schema\\n5. `unfold.go:Unfold()` expands value validations (anyOf, allOf etc.)\\n6. For v2: `v2/conversion.go:ToStructuralOpenAPIV2()` strips v2-incompatible constructs, then `kubeopenapi.go:ToKubeOpenAPI()` converts to go-openapi spec.Schema\\n7. `builder/builder.go:BuildOpenAPIV2()` / `BuildOpenAPIV3()` build full OpenAPI swagger/spec3 documents using kube-openapi builders\\n8. `builder/merge.go:MergeSpecs()` / `MergeSpecsV3()` merge per-CRD specs with the static built-in spec\\n9. `controller/openapi/controller.go:updateSpecLocked()` calls `openAPIService.UpdateSpecLazy()` to publish merged v2 spec\\n10. `controller/openapiv3/controller.go:updateGroupVersion()` calls `openAPIV3Service.UpdateGroupVersion()` to publish merged v3 spec per group/version\\n11. `apiserver/apiserver.go` starts both controllers as post-start hooks, connecting them to `OpenAPIVersionedService` and `OpenAPIV3VersionedService` which serve `/openapi/v2` and `/openapi/v3` endpoints\\n\"\n}\n",

Structural Schema Extraction\\n\\nThe structural schema package converts the JSONSchemaProps to an internal Structural representation:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/structural.go` \u2014 defines the `Structural` type\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/convert.go` \u2014 implements `NewStructural()` which converts `apiextensions.JSONSchemaProps` to `*Structural`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/validation.go` \u2014 implements `ValidateStructural()` which validates the structural schema\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/unfold.go` \u2014 implements `Unfold()` which expands ValueValidation (anyOf/allOf)\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/complete.go` \u2014 schema completion logic\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/skeleton.go` \u2014 structural skeleton construction\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/visitor.go` \u2014 visitor pattern for traversing structural schemas\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/schema/kubeopenapi.go` \u2014 implements `ToKubeOpenAPI()` which converts a `Structural` back to a go-openapi `spec.Schema`\\n\\n## 3. OpenAPI V3 and V2 Schema Conversion\\n\\nThe conversion from Structural schema to OpenAPI spec is done in the builder:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapi/builder/builder.go` \u2014 contains `generateBuilder()`, `BuildOpenAPIV2()`, and `BuildOpenAPIV3()`. The `generateBuilder` function calls `apiextensionshelpers.GetSchemaForVersion()` to get the CRD schema, converts it to internal form, calls `NewStructural()`, then `Unfold()`, and optionally strips value validations. `BuildOpenAPIV2` and `BuildOpenAPIV3` then produce OpenAPI specs from the restful routes and schema.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapi/v2/conversion.go` \u2014 implements `ToStructuralOpenAPIV2()` which strips OpenAPI v2-incompatible fields (allOf, oneOf, anyOf, not, nullable, etc.) from the structural schema before calling `ToKubeOpenAPI()`.\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapi/builder/merge.go` \u2014 implements `MergeSpecs()` (v2) and `MergeSpecsV3()` (v3) for merging per-version CRD specs together and with the static spec.\\n\\n## 4. API Server Spec Endpoint Publication\\n\\nThe controllers watch CRD changes and publish the OpenAPI specs:\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapi/controller.go` \u2014 `Controller` (v2): watches CRD informer, calls `BuildOpenAPIV2` per version, merges specs, and calls `openAPIService.UpdateSpecLazy(cache)` to publish to the `/openapi/v2` endpoint\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapi/metrics.go` \u2014 metrics for OpenAPI v2 regeneration\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapiv3/controller.go` \u2014 `Controller` (v3): watches CRD informer, calls `BuildOpenAPIV3` per version, merges specs per GroupVersion, and calls `openAPIV3Service.UpdateGroupVersion(path, mergedSpec)` to publish to the `/openapi/v3` endpoint\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapiv3/metrics.go` \u2014 metrics for OpenAPI v3 regeneration\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/openapiv3/util.go` \u2014 utility for converting GroupVersion to OpenAPI v3 path (`apis/<group>/<version>`)\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/controller/nonstructuralschema/nonstructuralschema_controller.go` \u2014 watches CRDs and sets the `NonStructuralSchema` condition, which gates OpenAPI publishing\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/apiserver.go` \u2014 wires everything together in the `start-apiextensions-controllers` post-start hook, launching both the v2 and v3 OpenAPI controllers using `GenericAPIServer.OpenAPIVersionedService` and `GenericAPIServer.OpenAPIV3VersionedService`\\n- `staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go` \u2014 uses structural schema for validation and schema-aware serving of custom resources\\n\\n## Complete Chain Summary\\n\\n1. `CustomResourceValidation.OpenAPIV3Schema` (in CRD spec, `v1/types.go`) is the input\\n2. `validation.go:ValidateCRDSpec()` validates the CRD including schema constraints (structural, types, CEL rules)\\n3. `convert.go:NewStructural()` converts `JSONSchemaProps` to `*Structural` (the internal structural representation)\\n4. `validation.go:ValidateStructural()` confirms it is a valid structural schema\\n5. `unfold.go:Unfold()` expands value validations (anyOf, allOf etc.)\\n6. For v2: `v2/conversion.go:ToStructuralOpenAPIV2()` strips v2-incompatible constructs, then `kubeopenapi.go:ToKubeOpenAPI()` converts to go-openapi spec.Schema\\n7. `builder/builder.go:BuildOpenAPIV2()` / `BuildOpenAPIV3()` build full OpenAPI swagger/spec3 documents using kube-openapi builders\\n8. `builder/merge.go:MergeSpecs()` / `MergeSpecsV3()` merge per-CRD specs with the static built-in spec\\n9. `controller/openapi/controller.go:updateSpecLocked()` calls `openAPIService.UpdateSpecLazy()` to publish merged v2 spec\\n10. `controller/openapiv3/controller.go:updateGroupVersion()` calls `openAPIV3Service.UpdateGroupVersion()` to publish merged v3 spec per group/version\\n11. `apiserver/apiserver.go` starts both controllers as post-start hooks, connecting them to `OpenAPIVersionedService` and `OpenAPIV3VersionedService` which serve `/openapi/v2` and `/openapi/v3` endpoints\\n\"\n}\n",
